<h4> <span class="mw-headline" id="Pi.C3.A8ces_du_2e_ton">Pi√®ces du 2e ton</span></h4>
<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP253112" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_7">

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>The term ¬´Suite¬ª should not be applied to that collection of 80 organ pieces because the composer did not use it in his published collection. A player could choose amongst the pieces in one particular church tone to suit his needs.
</li></ul>
